Revision: 88
Author: mserebre
Date: 4:56:44 AM, Monday, May 17, 2010
Message:
The camera component is complete, the cameras are 90% done.

The Component creates 3 monitors, the first 2 you can cycle through manually by using f11 and f12, the third one cycles by itself, automatically.  you can have as many cameras as you want in the scene, and they can be placed anywhere you want on the map, the component will pick them all up.

Cameras have a on/off option that can be toggled, so after you say...shoot a camera, you can grab a pointer to it and do something like this"
CamPtr->SetPowerOn(false);   this will turn it off, and it will vanish from the screen....

to make a camera follow you, or some other object, you need to pass your UniqueID or the objects UniqueID to the cam. All Game objects and Game actors have them. You also need to grab a pointer to the cam and do something like this:
CamPtr->TrackActor(mTrackedActor->GetUniqueId());
CamPtr->TrackingOn(true);

this will make the camera follow anything....
----

Message:
VRSim Lab v1.1.6.0226

updated the Content folder...

removed the Awing...

merged some of Albertos code into the master copy...

fixed a randomization bug in the ray casting...now the rays are cast every 2 sec, but at random time for each actor. before the randomization was from 0-2sec but what ever num u'd get was the loop length. so some actors would cast every 2 sec and some ever 0.001 of a sec...

Max amount of babies is now set through stage, not through code

Birth Rate is now set through stage

HappySpheres initial speed is now through stage

Ability to make the collision volume visible is now done through stage...

Path shortening is enabled and disabled through stage now

removed a lot of unnecessary variable passes
and slimmed down some functions...

Changes how proxies are done....to a more current way...

removed the animation from turns... it seems there is a bug somewhere in it(im still tracking it)... just to make sure its not messing up the collision avoidance i added 2 more turn functions that do an instant turn, all you need to supply are the degrees.

Message:
VRSim Lab v1.1.6.0226

updated the Content folder...

removed the Awing...

merged some of Albertos code into the master copy...

fixed a randomization bug in the ray casting...now the rays are cast every 2 sec, but at random time for each actor. before the randomization was from 0-2sec but what ever num u'd get was the loop length. so some actors would cast every 2 sec and some ever 0.001 of a sec...

Max amount of babies is now set through stage, not through code

Birth Rate is now set through stage

HappySpheres initial speed is now through stage

Ability to make the collision volume visible is now done through stage...

Path shortening is enabled and disabled through stage now

removed a lot of unnecessary variable passes
and slimmed down some functions...

Changes how proxies are done....to a more current way...

removed the animation from turns... it seems there is a bug somewhere in it(im still tracking it)... just to make sure its not messing up the collision avoidance i added 2 more turn functions that do an instant turn, all you need to supply are the degrees.

Revision: 60
Author: mserebre
Date: 8:03:49 PM, Wednesday, April 21, 2010
Message:
removed the Awing...

merged some of Albertos code into the master copy...

fixed a randomization bug in the ray casting...now the rays are cast every 2 sec, but at random time for each actor. before the randomization was from 0-2sec but what ever num u'd get was the loop length. so some actors would cast every 2 sec and some ever 0.001 of a sec...

Max amount of babies is now set through stage, not through code

Birth Rate is now set through stage

HappySpheres initial speed is now through stage

Ability to make the collision volume visible is now done through stage...

Path shortening is enabled and disabled through stage now

removed a lot of unnecessary variable passes
and slimmed down some functions...

Changes how proxies are done....to a more current way...

removed the animation from turns... it seems there is a bug somewhere in it(im still tracking it)... just to make sure its not messing up the collision avoidance i added 2 more turn functions that do an instant turn, all you need to supply are the degrees.
